<h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="General_Information">General Information</span></h2>
<div class="wi_body" style="width:100%">
<table border="0">

<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Work Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head" style="width:100%">Practische Orgelschule
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Alt<span class="mh555">ernative</span><span class="ms555">.</span> Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head">Practical Organ School
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composer
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Rinck,_Christian_Heinrich" title="Category:Rinck, Christian Heinrich">Rinck, Christian Heinrich</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Opus/Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">Op./Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>Op.55
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">I-Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">I-Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>ICR 17
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>6 volumes (Pieces numbered according to the W. T. Best edition)
<ul><li>Volume I
</li></ul>
<dl><dd>1-12. 12 Short and Easy Pieces in two parts
</dd><dd>13-24. 12 Short and Easy Pieces in three parts
</dd><dd>25-36. 12 Short and Easy Pieces in four parts
</dd><dd>37-66. 30 Preludes in all the major and minor keys
</dd></dl>
<ul><li>Volume II
</li></ul>
<dl><dd>67-132. 65 Short Pedal Exercises
</dd><dd>12 Chorales with variations
<dl><dd>133. Nun sich der Tag geendet hat
</dd><dd>134. Nun ruhen alle Wälder
</dd><dd>135. Mache dich mein Geist bereit
</dd><dd>136. Wer nur den lieben Gott lässt walten 
</dd><dd>137. Wie schön leucht der Morgenstern
</dd><dd>138. Freue dich sehr, o meine Seele
</dd><dd>139. Allein Gott in der Höh sey Ehr
</dd><dd>140. O Jesu Christ, meines Lebenslicht
</dd><dd>141. Auf Christenmensch, auf
</dd><dd>142. Wir glauben all’ an einen Gott
</dd><dd>143. Herr Jesu Christ dich zu uns wend
</dd><dd>144. Liebster Jesu wir sind hier
</dd></dl>
</dd></dl>
<ul><li>Volume III
</li></ul>
<dl><dd>145-159. 15 Easy Postludes in the Fugue Style
</dd></dl>
<ul><li>Volume IV
</li></ul>
<dl><dd>160-174. 15 Fugued Postludes for alternate manuals for more advanced players
</dd></dl>
<ul><li>Volume V
</li></ul>
<dl><dd>175-176. 2 Preludes
</dd><dd>177-180. 4 Postludes
</dd><dd>181. Fantasia <i>patetica</i> in E♭ minor/major
</dd><dd>182. Flute Concerto in F major
</dd><dd>183. Variations on 'God Save the King'
</dd></dl>
<ul><li>Volume VI
</li></ul>
<dl><dd>184-192. 6 Grand Preludes &amp; Fugues for more advanced players
</dd><dd>193-194. Fantasia &amp; Fugue in C minor
</dd><dd>195.  Prelude &amp; Fugue in B♭ major on B-A-C-H
</dd></dl>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>First Pub<span class="mh555">lication</span><span class="ms555">.</span>
</th>
<td>1820 or earlier
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Language
</th>
<td>German
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Composer Time Period</span><span class="ms555">Comp. Period</span>
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Classical" title="Category:Classical">Classical</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Piece Style
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Classical_style" title="Category:Classical style">Classical</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Instrumentation
</th>
<td>organ
</td></tr></table>
